## [Chris Batista](http://www.comicvine.com/chris-batista/4040-24182/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/0/1812/100556-85793-chris-batista.JPG" align="right" /> ##
American Comic book artist who worked on Steel, titans, wonder woman and JLA.

## [Jerry Bingham](http://www.comicvine.com/jerry-bingham/4040-4506/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/6/64770/1787399-jerry_bingham.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Jerry Bingham is an award winning comic book artist, he has worked for both of the "Big 2" in Marvel and DC Comics. His most well known and recognized artwork is in the Batman: Son of a Demon graphic novel, as well as Marvel Team-Up.

## [Eric Canete](http://www.comicvine.com/eric-canete/4040-46910/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/8/83392/1640257-173427_1010875550_1263045_n.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Eric Canete is an illustrator, designer and storyboard artist based in Los Angeles, CA. Comics work includes Cybernary 2.0, Iron Man: Enter The Mandarin, The End League, Luke Cage, Spider-man and Superboy.

## [Jim Cheung](http://www.comicvine.com/jim-cheung/4040-2256/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/0/77/254583-25334-jim-cheung.jpg" align="right" /> ##

## [Tony DeZuniga](http://www.comicvine.com/tony-dezuniga/4040-16372/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/2/28071/932008-tonydezuniga.jpg" align="right" /> ##
A Filipino comic-book artist. He worked with both Marvel and DC Comics, where he co-created the characters Jonah Hex and Black Orchid.


* [Action Comics Weekly (1988)](http://www.comicvine.com/action-comics-weekly/4050-3973/) 601-612, 618, 620-621, 623 (inker)

## [Tess Fowler](http://www.comicvine.com/tess-fowler/4040-58976/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/6/63017/1167293-tess.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Tess Fowler is a comic book illustrator based in California. To date she has worked on Michelle Obama Year One, Wonderland Annual 2010, Grimm Fairy Tales #54 and Charmed Issue #6. Her credits also include Heavy Metal Magazine and multiple sketch card projects. www.tessfowler.com

## [Ramona Fradon](http://www.comicvine.com/ramona-fradon/4040-33524/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/2/27783/1097075-ramona_fradon.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Under appreciated female pioneer artist in the male dominated comic book industry.  One of the first females to draw Superheroes in comic books!  Ms. Fradon worked on Aquaman &amp; is credited as co-creator of Metamorpho. Working through the Golden, Silver, Bronze and Modern-Age of comics.

## [Agnes Garbowska](http://www.comicvine.com/agnes-garbowska/4040-58854/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/0/40/2000131-photo_on_2011_09_06_at_21.jpeg" align="right" /> ##

## [Mick Gray](http://www.comicvine.com/mick-gray/4040-1252/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/0/9241/386202-80098-mick-gray.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Michael Gray is a comic book Inker. He is best known for his frequent collaborations with artist JH Williams III on titles such as Promethea and Chase, and with artist Patrick Gleason on Batman and Robin for DC Comics. He has been nominated a few times for "Best Inker" at the Harvey Awards.

## [Scott Hampton](http://www.comicvine.com/scott-hampton/4040-4505/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/0/9116/686522-scott_hampton___lucifer_miniserie_n.3_cover.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Comic book artist known for his iconic paintings. He is the brother of Bo Hampton.

## [Rob Liefeld](http://www.comicvine.com/rob-liefeld/4040-5181/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/4/40095/863187-robliefeld.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Rob Liefeld is a talented man. A comic book penciller, writer, and creator who rose to record-breaking success in the 1990's with titles such as The New Mutants, X-Force, and Youngblood. Liefeld is truly a prolific talent, and in many ways represents everything that is wrong with comics today.

## [Bill Maus](http://www.comicvine.com/bill-maus/4040-49184/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/1/15238/1271431-bill_maus_02.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Bill Maus is an independent small press comic book artist/ creator best known for his run on Zen: Intergalactic Ninja, Nira-X: Cyberangel and The Skunk for Comic Book publishers such as Avatar Press, Zen Comics, Entity Comics and many more.

## [Danny Miki](http://www.comicvine.com/danny-miki/4040-1922/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/6/66303/2878684-danny_miki_2010_wizard_anaheim_convention_0actzh.jpeg" align="right" /> ##

## [Todd Nauck](http://www.comicvine.com/todd-nauck/4040-9641/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/0/40/2688963-34770457841.jpeg" align="right" /> ##
Todd's been drawing comics since the early 90s and has published work with all the major companies including Marvel, DC, Dark Horse, and Image. 

Many associate him with Spider-Man but you never see them in the same place together.

* [52 (2006)](http://www.comicvine.com/52/4050-18053/) 11, 13 (artist, penciler)

## [Brandon Peterson](http://www.comicvine.com/brandon-peterson/4040-2204/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/3/31666/2927870-brandonpeterson.jpeg" align="right" /> ##

## [Richard Pini](http://www.comicvine.com/richard-pini/4040-19983/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/0/4/96132-73420-richard-pini.jpg" align="right" /> ##

## [Wendy Pini](http://www.comicvine.com/wendy-pini/4040-1547/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/0/40/726849-pini.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Wendy is a writer, artist and the co-creator of ElfQuest, the longest-running independant comic book series. Together with Richard Pini she is part of the creative team behind WaRP Graphics.

## [Whilce Portacio](http://www.comicvine.com/whilce-portacio/4040-6024/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/6/64770/2070498-whilce_portacio.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Filipino/American Comic book artist who has worked for Marvel, DC, and Image. Portacio was one of the original 7 founders of Image Comics.   He is also the creator of a number of big characters-including the X-men favorite Bishop.

## [Livio Ramondelli](http://www.comicvine.com/livio-ramondelli/4040-58322/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/0/9055/1039419-green_lantern_by_livio27.jpg" align="right" /> ##
Livio Ramondelli is a concept artist who currently works for DC/Wildstorm. Although he is a penciler he is known to often use paints and pastels for finished pieces.

## [Norm Rapmund](http://www.comicvine.com/norm-rapmund/4040-3761/) <img src="http://static.comicvine.com/uploads/square_avatar/1/15776/692131-norm.png" align="right" /> ##
Norm Rapmund is a comic book illusrator. He's drawn characters from Image, Marvel, and DC comics.
